\subsection{Detailed Description}
Author\-: Matthew Horridge\par
 The University Of Manchester\par
 Bio-\/\-Health Informatics Group\par
 Date\-: 06-\/\-Dec-\/2006\par
\par
 An abstract translator that can produce an R\-D\-F graph from an O\-W\-L\-Ontology. Subclasses must provide implementations to create concrete representations of resources, triples etc. 
\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em $<$\-N\-O\-D\-E$>$} & the basic node \\
\hline
{\em $<$\-R\-E\-S\-O\-U\-R\-C\-E$>$} & a resource node \\
\hline
{\em $<$\-P\-R\-E\-D\-I\-C\-A\-T\-E$>$} & a predicate node \\
\hline
{\em $<$\-L\-I\-T\-E\-R\-A\-L$>$} & a literal node \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}

\subsubsection[{add\-Pairwise\-Class\-Expressions}]{\setlength{\rightskip}{0pt plus 5cm}void org.\-coode.\-owlapi.\-rdf.\-model.\-Abstract\-Translator$<$ N\-O\-D\-E, R\-E\-S\-O\-U\-R\-C\-E extends N\-O\-D\-E, P\-R\-E\-D\-I\-C\-A\-T\-E extends N\-O\-D\-E, L\-I\-T\-E\-R\-A\-L extends N\-O\-D\-E $>$.add\-Pairwise\-Class\-Expressions (
\begin{DoxyParamCaption}
\item[{O\-W\-L\-Axiom}]{axiom, }
\item[{Set$<$ O\-W\-L\-Class\-Expression $>$}]{class\-Expressions, }
\item[{{\bf I\-R\-I}}]{I\-R\-I}
\end{DoxyParamCaption}
)\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [private]}}}\label{classorg_1_1coode_1_1owlapi_1_1rdf_1_1model_1_1_abstract_translator_3_01_n_o_d_e_00_01_r_e_s_o_ubc597564c2cb8c8d2b0139cb32f3f91c_ab3c9f86a9c855df45bfedc40b924aeb5}
Renders a set of class expressions in a pairwise manner using the specified I\-R\-I. It is assumed that the relationship described by the I\-R\-I (e.\-g. disjoint\-With) is symmetric. The method delegates to the {\ttfamily add\-Pairwise} method after sorting the class expressions so that named classes appear first. 
\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em axiom} & The axiom which will dictate which axiom annotation get rendered \\
\hline
{\em class\-Expressions} & The set of class expressions to be rendered. \\
\hline
{\em I\-R\-I} & The I\-R\-I which describes the relationship between pairs of class expressions. \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}

\begin{DoxyParamCaption}
\item[{O\-W\-L\-Axiom}]{ax, }
\item[{R\-E\-S\-O\-U\-R\-C\-E}]{subject, }
\item[{P\-R\-E\-D\-I\-C\-A\-T\-E}]{predicate, }
\item[{N\-O\-D\-E}]{object}
\end{DoxyParamCaption}
)\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [private]}}}\label{classorg_1_1coode_1_1owlapi_1_1rdf_1_1model_1_1_abstract_translator_3_01_n_o_d_e_00_01_r_e_s_o_ubc597564c2cb8c8d2b0139cb32f3f91c_a4a3089b09b9d529dec2494d10e327c02}
Adds the representation of an axiom to the R\-D\-F graph where the axiom has a S\-I\-N\-G\-L\-E M\-A\-I\-N T\-R\-I\-P\-L\-E (specified by the subject, predicate, object parameters). The triple specified by the subject, predicate and object parameters will be added to the graph. If the axiom has any annotations on it then extra triples will be added. These will consist of three triples, that \char`\"{}reify\char`\"{} (not in the R\-D\-F sense) the specified triple using the O\-W\-L 2 annotation vocabulary\-: owl\-:annotated\-Source, owl\-:annotated\-Property, owl\-:annotated\-Target, and other triples to encode the annotations. 
\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em ax} & The axiom that the triple specified as subject, pred, obj represents. \\
\hline
{\em subject} & The subject of the triple representing the axiom \\
\hline
{\em predicate} & The predicate of the triple representing the axiom \\
\hline
{\em object} & The object of the triple representing the axiom \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\hypertarget{classorg_1_1coode_1_1owlapi_1_1rdf_1_1model_1_1_abstract_translator_3_01_n_o_d_e_00_01_r_e_s_o_ubc597564c2cb8c8d2b0139cb32f3f91c_a212ec683d19a8dcb9c86c5aea10a6900}{\index{org\-::coode\-::owlapi\-::rdf\-::model\-::\-Abstract\-Translator$<$ N\-O\-D\-E, R\-E\-S\-O\-U\-R\-C\-E extends N\-O\-D\-E, P\-R\-E\-D\-I\-C\-A\-T\-E extends N\-O\-D\-E, L\-I\-T\-E\-R\-A\-L extends N\-O\-D\-E $>$@{org\-::coode\-::owlapi\-::rdf\-::model\-::\-Abstract\-Translator$<$ N\-O\-D\-E, R\-E\-S\-O\-U\-R\-C\-E extends N\-O\-D\-E, P\-R\-E\-D\-I\-C\-A\-T\-E extends N\-O\-D\-E, L\-I\-T\-E\-R\-A\-L extends N\-O\-D\-E $>$}!add\-Strong\-Typing@{add\-Strong\-Typing}}

\end{DoxyParamCaption}

Adds triples to strong type an entity. Triples are only added if the use\-Strong\-Typing flag is set to {\ttfamily true} and the entity is not a built in entity. 
\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}

\end{DoxyParams}
